<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Academy Award for Best Cinematography</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><table class="infobox vevent" style="width:22em">

</tr>

<p>The <b>Academy Award for Best Cinematography</b> is an <a href="/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="Academy Awards">Academy Award</a> awarded each year to a <a href="/wiki/Cinematographer" title="Cinematographer">cinematographer</a> for work on one particular <a href="/wiki/Film" title="Film">motion picture</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Academy_Award_for_Best_Cinematography&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div style="width:52px"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg"><img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/></a></div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>. <span class="hide-when-compact">Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Academy_Award_for_Best_Cinematography&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span> <small><i>(March 2010)</i></small> <small class="hide-when-compact"><i>(<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:282px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CharlesRosher.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="394" data-file-width="523" height="211" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4e/CharlesRosher.jpg/280px-CharlesRosher.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4e/CharlesRosher.jpg/420px-CharlesRosher.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/4/4e/CharlesRosher.jpg 2x" width="280"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:CharlesRosher.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Charles_Rosher" title="Charles Rosher">Charles Rosher</a>, the first recipient in 1928</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In its first film season, 1927–28, this award (like others such as the acting awards) was not tied to a specific film; all of the work by the nominated cinematographers during the qualifying period was listed after their names. The problem with this system became obvious the first year, since <a href="/wiki/Karl_Struss" title="Karl Struss">Karl Struss</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charles_Rosher" title="Charles Rosher">Charles Rosher</a> were nominated for their work together on <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sunrise_(film)" title="Sunrise (film)">Sunrise</a></i> but three other films shot individually by either Rosher or Struss were also listed as part of the nomination. The second year, 1929, there were no nominations at all, although the Academy has a list of unofficial titles which were under consideration by the Board of Judges. In the third year, 1930, films, not cinematographers, were nominated, and the final award did not show the cinematographer's name.</p>
<p>Finally, for the 1931 awards, the modern system in which individuals are nominated for a single film each was adopted in all profession-related categories. From 1939 to 1967 (with the single exception of 1957), there were also separate awards for color and for black-and-white cinematography. Since then, the only black-and-white film to win is <i><a href="/wiki/Schindler%27s_List" title="Schindler's List">Schindler's List</a></i> (1993).</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Floyd_Crosby" title="Floyd Crosby">Floyd Crosby</a> won the award for <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tabu_(1931_film)" title="Tabu (1931 film)">Tabu</a></i> in 1931, which was the last silent film to win in this category. <a href="/wiki/Hal_Mohr" title="Hal Mohr">Hal Mohr</a> won the only write-in Academy Award ever, in 1935 for <i><a href="/wiki/A_Midsummer_Night%27s_Dream_(1935_film)" title="A Midsummer Night's Dream (1935 film)">A Midsummer Night's Dream</a></i>. Mohr was also the first person to win for both black-and-white and color cinematography.</p>
<p>No winners are <a href="/wiki/Lost_film" title="Lost film">lost</a>, although some of the earliest nominees (and of the unofficial nominees of 1928–29) are lost, including <i><a href="/wiki/The_Devil_Dancer" title="The Devil Dancer">The Devil Dancer</a></i> (1927), <i><a href="/wiki/The_Magic_Flame" title="The Magic Flame">The Magic Flame</a></i> (1927), and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Four_Devils" title="Four Devils">Four Devils</a></i> (1928). <i><a href="/wiki/The_Right_to_Love_(1930_US_film)" title="The Right to Love (1930 US film)">The Right to Love</a></i> (1930) is incomplete, and <i><a href="/wiki/Sadie_Thompson" title="Sadie Thompson">Sadie Thompson</a></i> (1927) is incomplete and partially reconstructed with stills.</p>
<p>The first nominees shot primarily on <a href="/wiki/Digital_video" title="Digital video">digital video</a> were <i><a href="/wiki/The_Curious_Case_of_Benjamin_Button_(film)" title="The Curious Case of Benjamin Button (film)">The Curious Case of Benjamin Button</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Slumdog_Millionaire" title="Slumdog Millionaire">Slumdog Millionaire</a></i> in 2009, with <i>Slumdog Millionaire</i> the first winner.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> The following year <i><a href="/wiki/Avatar_(2009_film)" title="Avatar (2009 film)">Avatar</a></i> was the first nominee and winner to be shot entirely on digital video.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2017 a woman has never been nominated Best Cinematography, making it the only category<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> to have never nominated a woman.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></p>

<th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="background: #EEDD82">1928–1940</th>

<li><a href="/wiki/Joseph_T._Rucker" title="Joseph T. Rucker">Joseph T. Rucker</a> and <a href="/wiki/Willard_Van_der_Veer" title="Willard Van der Veer">Willard Van der Veer</a> (1930)</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/George_Barnes_(cinematographer)" title="George Barnes (cinematographer)">George Barnes</a> / <a href="/wiki/Georges_P%C3%A9rinal" title="Georges Périnal">George Perinal</a> (1940)</li>

<tr>
<th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="background: #EEDD82">1941–1960</th>
<td class="navbox-list navbox-even" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arthur_Miller_(cinematographer)" title="Arthur Miller (cinematographer)">Arthur C. Miller</a> / <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Palmer_(American_cinematographer)" title="Ernest Palmer (American cinematographer)">Ernest Palmer</a> (1941)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joseph_Ruttenberg" title="Joseph Ruttenberg">Joseph Ruttenberg</a> / <a href="/wiki/Leon_Shamroy" title="Leon Shamroy">Leon Shamroy</a> (1942)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arthur_Miller_(cinematographer)" title="Arthur Miller (cinematographer)">Arthur C. Miller</a> / <a href="/wiki/Hal_Mohr" title="Hal Mohr">Hal Mohr</a> (1943)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joseph_LaShelle" title="Joseph LaShelle">Joseph LaShelle</a> / <a href="/wiki/Leon_Shamroy" title="Leon Shamroy">Leon Shamroy</a> (1944)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Harry_Stradling" title="Harry Stradling">Harry Stradling</a> / <a href="/wiki/Leon_Shamroy" title="Leon Shamroy">Leon Shamroy</a> (1945)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arthur_Miller_(cinematographer)" title="Arthur Miller (cinematographer)">Arthur C. Miller</a> / <a href="/wiki/Charles_Rosher" title="Charles Rosher">Charles Rosher</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leonard_Smith_(cinematographer)" title="Leonard Smith (cinematographer)">Leonard Smith</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Arling" title="Arthur Arling">Arthur Arling</a> (1946)</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Burnett_Guffey" title="Burnett Guffey">Burnett Guffey</a> / <a href="/wiki/Loyal_Griggs" title="Loyal Griggs">Loyal Griggs</a> (1953)</li>
